DROP SEQUENCE MNO;
DROP SEQUENCE PNO;
DROP SEQUENCE BNO;
DROP SEQUENCE CNO;
DROP SEQUENCE NNO;
DROP SEQUENCE SNO;
DROP SEQUENCE RNO;
DROP SEQUENCE DNO;


SET PAGES 200;

-----------------------테이블생성시작--------------
-----------------------TABLE MEMBER--------------
ALTER TABLE MEMBER
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_MEM;

/* 회원 */
DROP TABLE MEMBER 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 회원 */
CREATE TABLE MEMBER (
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 회원번호 */
	id VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 아이디 */
	pw VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 비밀번호 */
	name VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 이름 */
	nick VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 닉네임 */
	birth NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 주민등록번호앞 */
	sex NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 주민등록번호뒤 */
	addr VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL /* 주소 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE MEMBER IS '회원';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.mno IS '회원번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.id IS '아이디';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.pw IS '비밀번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.name IS '이름';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.nick IS '닉네임';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.birth IS '주민등록번호앞';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.sex IS '주민등록번호뒤';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MEMBER.addr IS '주소';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_MEM
	ON MEMBER (
		mno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE MEMBER
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_MEM
		PRIMARY KEY (
			mno
		);
--Unique 조건 부여

ALTER TABLE member
     ADD CONSTRAINT id_only UNIQUE (id);

ALTER TABLE member
     ADD CONSTRAINT nick_only UNIQUE (nick);


--------------------------TABLE DETAIL-----------------------------
ALTER TABLE DETAIL
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_DET
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE DETAIL
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_DET;

/* 회원 추가정보 */
DROP TABLE DETAIL 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 회원 추가정보 */
CREATE TABLE DETAIL (
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 회원번호 */
	gender VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 성별 */
	age NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 연령대 */
	job VARCHAR2(100), /* 직업 */
	hobby VARCHAR2(200), /* 취미 */
	joindate DATE NOT NULL, /* 가입일자 */
	outdate DATE /* 탈퇴일자 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE DETAIL IS '회원 추가정보';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.mno IS '회원번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.gender IS '성별';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.age IS '연령대';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.job IS '직업';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.hobby IS '취미';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.joindate IS '가입일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN DETAIL.outdate IS '탈퇴일자';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_DET
	ON DETAIL (
		mno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE DETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_DET
		PRIMARY KEY (
			mno
		);

ALTER TABLE DETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_DET
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		) ON DELETE CASCADE;


---------------------------TABLE CATEGORY-------------------------------
ALTER TABLE CATEGORY
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_CAT;

/* 카테고리 */
DROP TABLE CATEGORY 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 카테고리 */
CREATE TABLE CATEGORY (
	catid NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 카테고리명 */
	xcat VARCHAR2(1000), /* 대분류1 */
	lcat VARCHAR2(1000), /* 대분류2 */
	mcat VARCHAR2(1000), /* 중분류 */
	scat VARCHAR2(1000) /* 소분류 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE CATEGORY IS '카테고리';

COMMENT ON COLUMN CATEGORY.catid IS '카테고리명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN CATEGORY.xcat IS '대분류1';

COMMENT ON COLUMN CATEGORY.lcat IS '대분류2';

COMMENT ON COLUMN CATEGORY.mcat IS '중분류';

COMMENT ON COLUMN CATEGORY.scat IS '소분류';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_CAT
	ON CATEGORY (
		catid ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE CATEGORY
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_CAT
		PRIMARY KEY (
			catid
		);

---------------------------TABLE PRODUCT-------------------------------
ALTER TABLE PRODUCT
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_PDT;

/* 상품 */
DROP TABLE PRODUCT 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 상품 */
CREATE TABLE PRODUCT (
	pno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 상품번호 */
	pid VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL, /* 상품아이디 */
	pname VARCHAR2(1500) NOT NULL, /* 상품명 */
	phprice NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 상품최고가격 */
	plprice NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 상품최저가격 */
	pmall VARCHAR2(1500) NOT NULL, /* 판매처(name) */
	pmallurl VARCHAR2(1500) NOT NULL, /* 판매처(url) */
	pimg VARCHAR(1500), /* 상품이미지 */
	catid NUMBER, /* 카테고리명 */
	tags VARCHAR2(1000) /* 해쉬태그 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE PRODUCT IS '상품';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pno IS '상품번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pid IS '상품아이디';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pname IS '상품명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.phprice IS '상품최고가격';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.plprice IS '상품최저가격';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pmall IS '판매처(name)';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pmallurl IS '판매처(url)';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.pimg IS '상품이미지';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.catid IS '카테고리명';

COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.tags IS '해쉬태그';

--COMMENT ON COLUMN PRODUCT.cat IS '카테고리';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_PDT
	ON PRODUCT (
		pno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE PRODUCT
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_PDT
		PRIMARY KEY (
			pno
		);

ALTER TABLE PRODUCT
	ADD
		FOREIGN KEY (
			catid
		)
		REFERENCES CATEGORY (
			catid
		) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-------------------------TABLE RELAY-------------------------------
ALTER TABLE RELAY
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_REL
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE RELAY
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_REL;

/* 릴레이 */
DROP TABLE RELAY 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 릴레이 */
CREATE TABLE RELAY (
	rno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 릴레이번호 */
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 개설자 */
	rname VARCHAR2(100), /* 받는사람 */
	rage NUMBER, /* 나이 */
	rgender VARCHAR2(100), /* 성별 */
	rjob VARCHAR2(100), /* 직업 */
	rhobby VARCHAR2(100) /* 취미 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE RELAY IS '릴레이';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rno IS '릴레이번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.mno IS '개설자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rname IS '받는사람';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rage IS '나이';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rgender IS '성별';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rjob IS '직업';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RELAY.rhobby IS '취미';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_REL
	ON RELAY (
		rno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE RELAY
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_REL
		PRIMARY KEY (
			rno
		);

ALTER TABLE RELAY
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_REL
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

--------------------------TABLE RDETAIL--------------------------------
ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_RDET
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_PRD_TO_RDET
		CASCADE;

	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_REL_TO_RDET
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_RDET;

/* 릴레이 상세 */
DROP TABLE RDETAIL 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 릴레이 상세 */
CREATE TABLE RDETAIL (
	rno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 릴레이번호 */
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 회원번호 */
	pno NUMBER /* 상품번호 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE RDETAIL IS '릴레이 상세';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RDETAIL.rno IS '릴레이번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RDETAIL.mno IS '회원번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN RDETAIL.pno IS '상품번호';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_RDETAIL
	ON RDETAIL (
		rno ASC,
		mno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_RDET
		PRIMARY KEY (
			rno,
			mno
		);

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_RDET
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_PRD_TO_RDET
		FOREIGN KEY (
			pno
		)
		REFERENCES PRODUCT (
			pno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_REL_TO_RDET
		FOREIGN KEY (
			rno
		)
		REFERENCES RELAY (
			rno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;


-------------------------TABLE MESSAGE-------------------------------

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_MSG
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_MSG2
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_REL_TO_MSG
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_MSG;

/* 쪽지 */
DROP TABLE MESSAGE 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 쪽지 */
CREATE TABLE MESSAGE (
	sno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 쪽지번호 */
	mno1 NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 보내는이 */
	mno2 NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 받는이 */
	stitle VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL, /* 쪽지제목 */
	scontent VARCHAR2(2000) NOT NULL, /* 쪽지내용 */
	sstate NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 상태 */
	sdate DATE NOT NULL, /* 쪽지작성일자 */
	svis NUMBER, /* VISIBILITY */
	restate NUMBER, /* 릴레이초대상태 */
	rno NUMBER /* 릴레이번호 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE MESSAGE IS '쪽지';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.sno IS '쪽지번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.mno1 IS '보내는이';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.mno2 IS '받는이';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.stitle IS '쪽지제목';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.scontent IS '쪽지내용';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.sstate IS '상태';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.sdate IS '쪽지작성일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.svis IS 'VISIBILITY';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.restate IS '릴레이초대상태';

COMMENT ON COLUMN MESSAGE.rno IS '릴레이번호';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_MSG
	ON MESSAGE (
		sno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_MSG
		PRIMARY KEY (
			sno
		);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_MSG
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno1
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_MSG2
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno2
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_REL_TO_MSG
		FOREIGN KEY (
			rno
		)
		REFERENCES RELAY (
			rno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;


------------------------------TABLE BOARD--------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE BOARD
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_BRD
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE BOARD
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_BRD;

/* 게시글 */
DROP TABLE BOARD 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 게시글 */
CREATE TABLE BOARD (
	bno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 게시글번호 */
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 회원번호 */
	btag VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 말머리태그 */
	btitle VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL, /* 게시글 제목 */
	bcontent VARCHAR2(2000) NOT NULL, /* 게시글 내용 */
	bimg VARCHAR2(1000), /* 이미지(name) */
	bimgurl VARCHAR2(1000), /* 이미지(url) */
	bdate DATE NOT NULL, /* 게시글작성일자 */
	bupdate DATE, /* 게시글수정일자 */
	bvis NUMBER NOT NULL, /* VISIBILITY */
	breplycnt NUMBER, /* 댓글갯수 */
	bcnt NUMBER NOT NULL /* 게시판조회수 */
);
COMMENT ON TABLE BOARD IS '게시글';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bno IS '게시글번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.mno IS '회원번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.btag IS '말머리태그';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.btitle IS '게시글 제목';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bcontent IS '게시글 내용';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bimg IS '이미지(name)';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bimgurl IS '이미지(url)';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bdate IS '게시글작성일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bupdate IS '게시글수정일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bvis IS 'VISIBILITY';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.breplycnt IS '댓글갯수';

COMMENT ON COLUMN BOARD.bcnt IS '게시판조회수';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_BRD
	ON BOARD (
		bno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE BOARD
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_BRD
		PRIMARY KEY (
			bno
		);

ALTER TABLE BOARD
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_BRD
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		) ON DELETE CASCADE;

---------------------------------TABLE COMM---------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE COMM
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_BRD_TO_COM
		CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE COMM
	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

DROP INDEX PK_COMM;

/* 댓글테이블 */
DROP TABLE COMM 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 댓글테이블 */
CREATE TABLE COMM (
	bno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 게시글번호 */
	cno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 댓글번호 */
	ccontent VARCHAR2(500) NOT NULL, /* 댓글내용 */
	creplyer VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL, /* 댓글작성자 */
	cdate DATE NOT NULL, /* 댓글작성일자 */
	cupdate DATE, /* 댓글수정일자 */
	cvis NUMBER NOT NULL, /* VISIBILITY */
	cdeldate NUMBER /* 댓글삭제일자 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE COMM IS '댓글테이블';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.bno IS '게시글번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.cno IS '댓글번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.ccontent IS '댓글내용';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.creplyer IS '댓글작성자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.cdate IS '댓글작성일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.cupdate IS '댓글수정일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.cvis IS 'VISIBILITY';

COMMENT ON COLUMN COMM.cdeldate IS '댓글삭제일자';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_COMM
	ON COMM (
		bno ASC,
		cno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE COMM
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_COMM
		PRIMARY KEY (
			bno,
			cno
		);

ALTER TABLE COMM
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_BRD_TO_COM
		FOREIGN KEY (
			bno
		)
		REFERENCES BOARD (
			bno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;


-------------------------------TABLE NOTICE--------------------------------------------
ALTER TABLE NOTICE
	DROP
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_NOT
		CASCADE;

	DROP
		PRIMARY KEY
		CASCADE
		KEEP INDEX;

/* 공지글 */
DROP TABLE NOTICE 
	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

/* 공지글 */
CREATE TABLE NOTICE (
	nno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 게시글번호 */
	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 관리자번호 */
	ntitle VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL, /* 게시글 제목 */
	ncontent VARCHAR2(2000) NOT NULL, /* 게시글 내용 */
	ndate DATE NOT NULL, /* 공지글작성일자 */
	nupdate DATE, /* 공지글수정일자 */
	nvis NUMBER NOT NULL, /* VISIBILITY */
	ncnt NUMBER NOT NULL /* 공지사항조회수 */
);

COMMENT ON TABLE NOTICE IS '공지글';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.nno IS '게시글번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.mno IS '관리자번호';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.ntitle IS '게시글 제목';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.ncontent IS '게시글 내용';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.ndate IS '공지글작성일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.nupdate IS '공지글수정일자';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.nvis IS 'VISIBILITY';

COMMENT ON COLUMN NOTICE.ncnt IS '공지사항조회수';

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX PK_NOT
	ON NOTICE (
		nno ASC
	);

ALTER TABLE NOTICE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT PK_NOT
		PRIMARY KEY (
			nno
		);

ALTER TABLE NOTICE
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_NOT
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

	CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

	mno NUMBER NOT NULL, /* 회원번호 */

);

COMMENT ON TABLE WISHLIST IS '위시리스트';

			mno,
			pno
		);

ALTER TABLE WISHLIST
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_MEM_TO_WISH
		FOREIGN KEY (
			mno
		)
		REFERENCES MEMBER (
			mno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE WISHLIST
	ADD
		CONSTRAINT FK_PRD_TO_WISH
		FOREIGN KEY (
			pno
		)
		REFERENCES PRODUCT (
			pno
		)ON DELETE CASCADE;

------------------------속성 DEFAULT 값 생성------------------------------
ALTER TABLE DETAIL MODIFY (JOINDATE DEFAULT SYSDATE);

ALTER TABLE PRODUCT MODIFY (TAGS DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE BOARD MODIFY (BDATE DEFAULT SYSDATE);

ALTER TABLE BOARD MODIFY (BVIS DEFAULT 1);

ALTER TABLE BOARD MODIFY (BREPLYCNT DEFAULT 0);

ALTER TABLE BOARD MODIFY (BCNT DEFAULT 0);

ALTER TABLE NOTICE MODIFY (NDATE DEFAULT SYSDATE);

ALTER TABLE NOTICE MODIFY (NVIS DEFAULT 1);

ALTER TABLE NOTICE MODIFY (NCNT DEFAULT 0);

ALTER TABLE COMM MODIFY (CDATE DEFAULT SYSDATE);

ALTER TABLE COMM MODIFY (CVIS DEFAULT 1);

ALTER TABLE WISHLIST MODIFY (PNICK DEFAULT '1');

ALTER TABLE RELAY MODIFY (RNAME DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE RELAY MODIFY (RAGE DEFAULT 0);

ALTER TABLE RELAY MODIFY (RGENDER DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE RELAY MODIFY (RJOB DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE RELAY MODIFY (RHOBBY DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE MODIFY (SSTATE DEFAULT 1);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE MODIFY (SDATE DEFAULT SYSDATE);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE MODIFY (SVIS DEFAULT 1);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE MODIFY (RESTATE DEFAULT 5);

ALTER TABLE MESSAGE MODIFY (RNO DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE WISHLIST MODIFY (grade DEFAULT '');

ALTER TABLE RDETAIL MODIFY (PNO DEFAULT '');


--------------------------테이블 체크 옵션--------------------------------------

ALTER TABLE MEMBER ADD CONSTRAINT SEX_CH CHECK(SEX IN (1,2,3,4) );

ALTER TABLE DETAIL ADD CONSTRAINT AGE_CH CHECK(AGE IN (10, 20, 30, 40, 50, 60));

ALTER TABLE BOARD ADD CONSTRAINT BVIS_CH CHECK(BVIS IN (0, 1));

ALTER TABLE NOTICE ADD CONSTRAINT NVIS_CH CHECK(NVIS IN (0, 1));

ALTER TABLE NOTICE ADD CONSTRAINT MNO_CH CHECK(MNO IN (1) );

ALTER TABLE COMM ADD CONSTRAINT CVIS_CH CHECK(CVIS IN (0, 1));

ALTER TABLE WISHLIST ADD CONSTRAINT GRADE_CH CHECK(GRADE IN (0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5));


----------------------SEQUENCE 생성------------------------------------

CREATE SEQUENCE MNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE PNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE BNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE CNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE NNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE SNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE RNO START WITH 1 INCREMENT BY 1 MAXVALUE 10000;

CREATE SEQUENCE DNO START WITH 11111111 INCREMENT BY 1;

-----------------------------테이블 구조 확인-----------------------------------

desc member;

desc detail;

desc product;

desc wishlist;

desc board;

desc comm;

desc notice;

-------------------------------프로시저----------------------------------------
-- 회원 정보 추가 프로시저 --
create or replace procedure MEM_INSERT(
mid in member.id%type, 
mpw in member.pw%type, 
mname in member.name%type,
mnick in member.nick%type, 
mbirth in member.birth%type, 
msex in member.sex%type, 
maddr in member.addr%type,
dgender in detail.gender%type,
dage in detail.age%type,
djob in detail.job%type, 
dhobby in detail.hobby%type
)
is
begin
insert into member(mno, id, pw, name, nick, birth, sex, addr)
values(mno.nextval, mid, mpw, mname, mnick, mbirth, msex, maddr);
insert into detail(mno, gender, age, job, hobby, joindate, outdate)
values(mno.currval, dgender, dage, djob, dhobby, default, '');
end MEM_INSERT;
/


-- 회원정보 수정 프로시저 --
create or replace procedure MEM_UPDATE(
mid in member.id%type,
mpw in member.pw%type,
mname in member.name%type,
maddr in member.addr%type,
djob in detail.job%type,
dhobby in detail.hobby%type
)
is
begin
update member set pw=mpw, name=mname, addr=maddr where id=mid;
update detail set job=djob, hobby=dhobby
where mno = (select mno from member where id=mid);
end MEM_UPDATE;
/

----------------트리거-----------------
-----------회원 탈퇴일자 수정 트리거-------------
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER OUTDATE_UP
AFTER
	UPDATE of BIRTH ON MEMBER
DECLARE
BEGIN
		UPDATE DETAIL
		SET OUTDATE = SYSDATE
		WHERE mno in (select mno from member where birth = 0) 
		and outdate is null;
END;
/

--------------탈퇴 회원 게시물 VIS 트리거------------
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER BOARD_UP
AFTER
	UPDATE of BIRTH ON MEMBER
DECLARE
BEGIN
		UPDATE BOARD
		SET BVIS = 0
		WHERE mno in (select mno from member where birth = 0) 
		and BVIS = 1;
END;
/

--------------탈퇴 회원 댓글 VIS 트리거 방법1 그냥 안보이게 하기-----------------

--------------탈퇴 회원 댓글 VIS 트리거 방법2 관리자로 작성자 바꾸고 내용 삭제된 회원이 작성한 댓글입니다로 변경-----------------
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER COMM_UP2
AFTER
	UPDATE of BIRTH ON MEMBER
DECLARE
BEGIN
	UPDATE COMM
	SET CREPLYER = 'admin'
	WHERE CREPLYER NOT IN (SELECT NICK FROM MEMBER);
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER COMM_UP3
AFTER
	UPDATE of BIRTH ON MEMBER
DECLARE
BEGIN
	UPDATE COMM
	SET CCONTENT = '삭제된 회원이 작성한 댓글입니다.'
	WHERE CREPLYER NOT IN (SELECT NICK FROM MEMBER);
END;
/
